## Configuration

### Excluded Patterns

The following are automatically excluded:

- `node_modules`
- `dist`
- `build`
- `.git`
- `coverage`
- `.next`
- `out`
- `__tests__`
- `vendor`
- `backup`
- `__pycache__`
- `target`
- `.venv`
- `venv`
- `tmp`
- `temp`
- `.cache`
- Hidden files and directories (starting with `.`)

### Settings

- **Root Directory:** `SimpleTool/`
- **Maximum Depth:** 7 levels
- **Output File:** `docs/project-structure.md`
